<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выстрел.html>вы́стрел</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výstrel</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выстрел.html>вы́стрела</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выстрел.html>вы́стрелы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выстрел.html>вы́стрелов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>shot, gunshot, round (launching of a projectile)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выстрелить.html>вы́стрелить</a> (4008)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-стрели́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-strelítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выстрелить.html>вы́стрелить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výstrelitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стрелять.html>стреля́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выстреливать.html>выстре́ливать</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выстроенный.html>вы́строенный</a> (6288)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выстроенный.html>вы́строенный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výstrojennyj</span>)
</p>

***выступ.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выступ.html>вы́ступ</a> (8657)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выступ.html>вы́ступ</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výstup</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выступ.html>вы́ступа</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выступ.html>вы́ступы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выступ.html>вы́ступов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>protrusion, protuberance, prominence, projection <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">anything that protrudes</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">cartography</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a panhandle</li>
<li>ledge</li></ol>

***выступать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выступать.html>выступа́ть</a> (1482)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ступать.html>ступа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stupátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выступать.html>выступа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vystupátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выступить.html>вы́ступить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to project, to protrude, to jut, to jut out, to come out, to stand out</li>
<li>to step forth, to step forward</li>
<li>to set out, to march off</li>
<li>to appear</li>
<li>to strut</li>
<li>to perform <i>at the scene</i></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ступить.html>ступи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stupítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выступить.html>вы́ступить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výstupitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выступать.html>выступа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to project, to protrude, to jut, to jut out, to come out, to stand out</li>
<li>to step forth, to step forward</li>
<li>to set out, to march off</li>
<li>to appear</li>
<li>to strut</li>
<li>to perform <i>at the scene</i></li></ol>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>своём</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:выступление.html>выступле́нии</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:докладчик.html>докла́дчик</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:осветить.html>освети́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ряд.html>ряд</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:международный.html>междунаро́дных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вопрос.html>вопро́сов</a>. </span></li>
</ul></li>

***высунуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:высунуть.html>вы́сунуть</a> (7314)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сунуть.html>су́нуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">súnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высунуть.html>вы́сунуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výsunutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высовывать.html>высо́вывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to put out, to stick out, to thrust out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:высунуть.html>вы́сунуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>язы́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výsunutʹ</b> jazýk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put/stick one's tongue out</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нельзя.html>нельзя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нос.html>но́су</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:высунуть.html>вы́сунуть</a></b> (<a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>до́му</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nelʹzjá nósu <b>výsunutʹ</b> (iz dómu)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">you can't even stick your nose out (of the house); you can't even show your face outside</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:высунуть.html>вы́сунув</a></b>/<b>вы́суня</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>язы́к</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:очень.html>о́чень</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быстро.html>бы́стро</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výsunuv</b>/<b>výsunja</b> jazýk (óčenʹ býstro)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">like mad; like a bat out of hell; with one's tongue hanging out</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:высушивать.html>высу́шивать</a> (28219)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высушить.html>вы́сушить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výsušitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высушивать.html>высу́шивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vysúšivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высушить.html>вы́сушить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dry</li>
<li>to roast, to toast, to parch</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wear out, to exhaust, to torment</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to harden <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">one's heart</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to make heartless</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:высушить.html>вы́сушить</a> (11503)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сушить.html>суши́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sušítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высушить.html>вы́сушить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výsušitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сушить.html>суши́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высушивать.html>высу́шивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dry</li>
<li>to roast, to toast, to parch</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wear out, to exhaust, to torment</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to harden <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">one's heart</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to make heartless</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:высчитавший.html>вы́считавший</a> (27947)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высчитавший.html>вы́считавший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výsčitavšij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высчитать.html>вы́считать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výsčitatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***высылать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:высылать.html>высыла́ть</a> (15534)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-сыла́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sylátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высылать.html>высыла́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vysylátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выслать.html>вы́слать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to send, to dispatch, to send forward</li>
<li>to banish, to exile; to deport, to expel</li></ol>

***высылка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:высылка.html>вы́сылка</a> (18713)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высылать.html>высыла́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vysylátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to dispatch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with stress based on perfective <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выслать.html>вы́слать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výslatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высылка.html>вы́сылка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výsylka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высылка.html>вы́сылки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высылка.html>вы́сылки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высылка.html>вы́сылок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>dispatch, sending</li>
<li>exile, banishment; deportation, expulsion; renvoi</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:высыпать.html>высыпа́ть</a> (7263)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыпать.html>сы́пать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sýpatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высыпать.html>вы́сыпать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výsypatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:высыпать.html>высыпа́ть</a></strong></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">the impf./pf. forms differ in the word stress in the infinitive and the conjugation</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>to strew out, to pour out, to empty <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to distribute objects or pieces of something</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to pour out, to throng <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a crowd</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to break out, to come out <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a rash, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
